cz_idk_category = {
	aha_idk = {
		icon = decision
		visible = {
			always = yes
		}
		available = {
			#always = yes
			always = no
		}
		cost = 0
		days_remove = 0
		days_re_enable = 0
	
		ai_will_do = { base = 0 }
	
		complete_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_idea = CZ_V4_member
						has_idea = CZ_V4_member_better
						has_idea = CZ_CEU_member
					}
					NOT = { original_tag = CZE }
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_temp_variable = { influence_gain = 2000 }
					for_loop_effect = {
						end = influence_array^num
						value = v
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { influence_array^v = CZE }
							}
							add_to_variable = { influence_array_val^v = influence_gain }
							set_country_flag = found
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = found } }
							add_to_array = { influence_array = CZE.id }
							add_to_array = { influence_array_val = influence_gain }
					}
					clr_country_flag = found
					recalculate_influence = yes
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = small_influence_40_tt
			}
			#remove_ideas = { CZ_leader_of_v4_idea }
		}
	}
	aha_idk2 = {
		icon = decision
		visible = {
			always = yes
		}
		available = {
			#always = yes
			always = no
		}
		cost = 0
		days_remove = 0
		days_re_enable = 0
	
		ai_will_do = { base = 0 }
	
		complete_effect = {
			add_ideas = { CZ_PP_cheat }
		}
	}

	cze_vs_slo = {
		icon = cze_vs_slo

		available = {
			has_government = nationalist
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						controls_state = 119
						119 = { 
							CONTROLLER = {
								is_subject_of = FROM
							}
						}

							CONTROLLER = {
								is_in_faction_with = FROM

				has_country_flag = czechia_cze_vs_slo_event

								is_subject_of = FROM		
							}
						}

							CONTROLLER = {
								FROM = {

										target = PREV
										type = take_state_focus

							}
						}

							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						120 = {
							CONTROLLER = {
								is_subject_of = FROM
							}
						}
						controls_state = 120	
					}
					OR = {
						controls_state = 119

								is_subject_of = FROM
							}
						}
					}
				}

    							target = PREV
    							generator = {120}
							}
						}
					}
				}

				limit = {

							CONTROLLER = {
								is_subject_of = FROM
							}
						}
						120 = {
							CONTROLLER = {
								is_subject_of = FROM
							}
						}
						controls_state = 119
						controls_state = 120	
					}
					119 = {
						CONTROLLER = {
							controls_state = 120
						}
					}
				}
				120 = { 
					CONTROLLER = {
						FROM = {
							create_wargoal = {
								type = take_state_focus
    							target = PREV
    							generator = {120}
								generator = {119}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						119 = {
							CONTROLLER = {
								is_subject_of = FROM
							}
						}

	czech_riots = {
    	icon = riots_dec

    	allowed = {
    		always = yes
    	}
    	available = {
			OR = {
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = czechia_decision_riots_tt
					has_country_flag = cz_riots_suppressed
				}
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = czechia_CCW_tt
					has_country_flag = Czech_Civil_War
				}
				has_completed_focus = czechia_focus_bannat
				has_completed_focus = czechia_focus_bancom
			}	
    	}
    	activation = {
			OR = {
				has_idea = CZE_riotscom
				has_idea = CZE_riotsnat
				has_idea = CZE_riotsfas
			}
    	}
    	fire_only_once = no
        days_mission_timeout = 90
        days_remove = 0
        ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = CZE_riotscom
				}
				remove_ideas = {
					CZE_riotscom
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = CZE_riotsnat
				}
				remove_ideas = {
					CZE_riotsnat
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = CZE_riotsfas
				}
				remove_ideas = {
					CZE_riotsfas
				}
			}
        }
        timeout_effect = {
        	if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = CZE_riotscom
				}
				remove_ideas = {
					CZE_riotscom
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = CZE_riotsnat
				}
				remove_ideas = {
					CZE_riotsnat
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = CZE_riotsfas
				}
				remove_ideas = {
					CZE_riotsfas
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Communist-State
						has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_anarchist_communism
						has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Conservative
						has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Autocracy
					}
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = Czech_Civil_War
					}
				}
				country_event = {
				    id = czechia.15
				    days = 2
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = nationalist
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = Czech_Civil_War
					}
				}
				country_event = {
				    id = czechia.18
				    days = 2
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = czechia_mas_imigration_on
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = Czech_Civil_War
					}
				}
				country_event = {
				    id = czechia.24
				    days = 2
				}
			}
        }
    }

	czech_islam_civ_fac = {

		icon = czechia_build_civ_dec

		available = {
			OR = {
				has_idea = CZE_secret_immigrants_coming	
				has_idea = CZE_immigrants_coming
			}
			has_full_control_of_state = 117
		}

		visible = {
			OR = {
				has_idea = CZE_secret_immigrants_coming	
				has_idea = CZE_immigrants_coming
			}
			NOT = {
				has_completed_focus = czechia_focus_fas6	
			}
			check_variable = { czechia_civ_factories < 5 }
		}

		cost = 100
		days_remove = 90
		days_re_enable = 1
		fire_only_once = no

		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = czechia_civ_factories
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { czechia_civ_factories < 5 }
					}
					add_to_variable = { czechia_civ_factories = 1 }
					add_to_variable = { czechia_civ_factories_minus = -1 }
					117 = {
						add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
						add_building_construction = {
							type = industrial_complex
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}

						limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = found } }
							add_to_array = { influence_array = CZE.id }
							add_to_array = { influence_array_val = influence_gain }
					}
					clr_country_flag = found
					recalculate_influence = yes
				}

			}

				hidden_effect = {
					set_temp_variable = { influence_gain = 250 }
					for_loop_effect = {
						end = influence_array^num
						value = v
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { influence_array^v = CZE }
							}
							add_to_variable = { influence_array_val^v = influence_gain }
							set_country_flag = found
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = found } }
							add_to_array = { influence_array = CZE.id }
							add_to_array = { influence_array_val = influence_gain }
					}
					clr_country_flag = found
					recalculate_influence = yes
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = small_influence_250_tt
			}
			complete_national_focus = EU002
			activate_decision = EU_apply_for_membership
		}

			factor = 200
			modifier = {

				}

					NOT = {

		}

	czech_visegrad_influence_pol = {

		icon = influence_dec

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = var:czechia_pol_capital
			}
			highlight_color_while_active = 4
		}


		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = czechia_is_leader_of_v4
				has_country_flag = official_leader_of_v4
			}
			POL = {
				has_opinion_modifier = v4_member_better_opinion
			}
			has_government = neutrality
			political_power_daily > 0.5
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = required_not_70_influence_pol
				POL = {
					OR = {
						tag = PREV
						AND = {
							set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
							any_of = {
								array = influence_array
								value = v
								index = i
								if = {
									limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
									set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
									always = yes
								}
								else = { always = no }
							}
							check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
							check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx < 0.70 }
						}
						NOT = {
							check_variable = { influence_array^0 = CZE }
							check_variable = { influence_array_calc^0 > 0.5 }

							check_variable = { influence_array^1 = CZE }
							check_variable = { influence_array_calc^1 > 0.5 }

							check_variable = { influence_array^2 = CZE }
							check_variable = { influence_array_calc^2 > 0.5 }

							check_variable = { influence_array^3 = CZE }
							check_variable = { influence_array_calc^3 > 0.5 }

							check_variable = { influence_array^4 = CZE }
							check_variable = { influence_array_calc^4 > 0.5 }

							check_variable = { influence_array^5 = CZE }
							check_variable = { influence_array_calc^5 > 0.5 }

							check_variable = { influence_array^6 = CZE }
							check_variable = { influence_array_calc^6 > 0.5 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			#POL = {
			#	
			#}
			country_exists = POL
		}

		visible = {
			POL = {
				has_opinion_modifier = v4_member_better_opinion
			}
			has_completed_focus = czechia_visegrad_convince
			country_exists = POL

				OR = {
					tag = PREV
					AND = {
						set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
						any_of = {
							array = influence_array
							value = v
							index = i
							if = {
								limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
								set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
								always = yes
							}
							else = { always = no }
						}

						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx < 0.70 }

							index = i
							if = {
								limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
								set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
								always = yes
							}
							else = { always = no }
						}
						check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx < 0.70 }
					}
					NOT = {
						check_variable = { influence_array^0 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^0 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^1 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^1 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^2 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^2 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^3 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^3 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^4 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^4 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^5 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^5 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^6 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^6 > 0.5 }
					}
				}
			}
			has_completed_focus = czechia_visegrad_convince
			country_exists = HUN
		}

		cost = 50
		days_remove = 20
		days_re_enable = 1
		fire_only_once = no

		modifier = {
            political_power_gain = -0.50
        }

		remove_effect = {
			HUN = {
				hidden_effect = {
					set_temp_variable = { influence_gain = 40 }
					for_loop_effect = {
						end = influence_array^num
						value = v
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { influence_array^v = CZE }
							}
							add_to_variable = { influence_array_val^v = influence_gain }
							set_country_flag = found
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = found } }
							add_to_array = { influence_array = CZE.id }
							add_to_array = { influence_array_val = influence_gain }
					}
					clr_country_flag = found
					recalculate_influence = yes
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = small_influence_40_tt
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 200
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_COMMUNIST
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_NATIONALIST
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_JIHADISTS
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_NEUTRALITY
				}
				factor = 5000
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = DEFAULT
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}

	czech_neu_create_fac_pol = {

		icon = faction_dec

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = var:czechia_pol_capital
			}
			highlight_color_while_active = 2
		}


		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = czechia_is_leader_of_v4
				has_country_flag = official_leader_of_v4
			}
			political_power_daily > 0.5
			has_government = neutrality
			POL = {
				has_opinion_modifier = v4_member_better_opinion
			}
			country_exists = POL
			POL = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = CZE_Czech_alliance
					has_war_with = FROM
					CZE = {
						has_wargoal_against = PREV
					}
				}
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = czechia_influence_above50_pol_tt
					OR = {
						tag = PREV
						AND = {
							set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
							any_of = {
								array = influence_array
								value = v
								index = i
								if = {
									limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
									set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
									always = yes
								}
								else = { always = no }
							}
							check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
							check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.50 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = czechia_visegrad_faction
			country_exists = POL
			POL = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = CZE_Czech_alliance
					has_war_with = FROM
					CZE = {
						has_wargoal_against = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}

		cost = 10
		days_remove = 20
		days_re_enable = 1
		fire_only_once = no

		modifier = {
            political_power_gain = -0.50
        }

		remove_effect = {
			POL = {
				country_event = { id = czechia.44 }	
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 200
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_COMMUNIST
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_JIHADISTS
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_NATIONALIST
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_NEUTRALITY
				}
				factor = 5000
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = DEFAULT
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}

	czech_puppet_pol = {

		icon = puppet_dec

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = var:czechia_pol_capital
			}
			highlight_color_while_active = 3
		}


		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = czechia_is_leader_of_v4
				has_country_flag = official_leader_of_v4
			}
			political_power_daily > 0.5
			POL = {
				has_opinion_modifier = v4_member_better_opinion
			}
			has_government = neutrality
			has_idea = CZE_Czech_alliance
			POL = {
				has_idea = CZE_Czech_alliance
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = CZE
					is_subject_of = CZE
				}
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = czechia_influence_above60_pol_tt
					OR = {
						tag = PREV
						AND = {
							set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
							any_of = {
								array = influence_array
								value = v
								index = i
								if = {
									limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
									set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
									always = yes
								}
								else = { always = no }
							}
							check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
							check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.60 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = czechia_visegrad_integrate
			has_idea = CZE_Czech_alliance
			country_exists = POL
			POL = {
				has_idea = CZE_Czech_alliance
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = CZE
					is_subject_of = CZE
				}
			}
		}

		cost = 10
		days_remove = 20
		days_re_enable = 1
		fire_only_once = no

		modifier = {
            political_power_gain = -0.50
        }

		remove_effect = {
			POL = {
				CZE = {
					puppet = PREV
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_opinion_modifier = v4_member_better_opinion
						}
					}
					POL = {
						add_opinion_modifier = {
						    target = FROM
						    modifier = v4_member_better_opinion
						}
					}
					add_opinion_modifier = {
					    target = POL
					    modifier = v4_member_better_opinion
					}
				}
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_COMMUNIST
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_JIHADISTS
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_NATIONALIST
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_NEUTRALITY
				}
				factor = 5000
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = DEFAULT
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}

        }

					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_JIHADISTS

	czech_visegrad_group = {

		icon = v4_dec

		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = czechia_is_leader_of_v4
				has_country_flag = official_leader_of_v4
			}
			political_power_daily > 2
			has_government = neutrality
			NOT = {
				country_exists = POL
				country_exists = HUN
				country_exists = SLO
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = czechia_all_v4_tt
				all_state = {
					OR = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = POL }
						AND = {
							is_core_of = POL
							owner = { tag = CZE }
						}
					}
				}
				all_state = {
					OR = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = HUN }
						AND = {
							is_core_of = HUN
							owner = { tag = CZE }
						}
					}
				}
				all_state = {
					OR = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = SLO }
						AND = {
							is_core_of = SLO
							owner = { tag = CZE }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = czechia_visegrad_integrate
			NOT = {
				has_cosmetic_tag = CZE_V4
			}
		}

		cost = 10
		days_remove = 20
		days_re_enable = 1
		fire_only_once = yes

		modifier = {
			political_power_gain = -2
		}

		remove_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = POL
				}
				add_core_of = CZE
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = HUN
				}
				add_core_of = CZE
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = SLO
				}
				add_core_of = CZE
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = CZE_V4
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 200
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_COMMUNIST
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_NATIONALIST
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_JIHADISTS
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_NEUTRALITY
				}
				factor = 5000
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = DEFAULT
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}

	czech_TSI_influence_est = {

		icon = influence_dec

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = var:czechia_est_capital
			}
			highlight_color_while_active = 4
		}


		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = czechia_is_leader_of_TSI
				has_country_flag = official_leader_of_TSI
			}
			EST = {
				has_opinion_modifier = threesi_member_modifier
			}
			has_government = neutrality
			political_power_daily > 0.5
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = required_not_70_influence_est
				EST = {
					OR = {
						tag = PREV
						AND = {
							set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
							any_of = {
								array = influence_array
								value = v
								index = i
								if = {
									limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
									set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
									always = yes
								}
								else = { always = no }
							}
							check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
							check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx < 0.70 }
						}
						NOT = {
							check_variable = { influence_array^0 = CZE }
							check_variable = { influence_array_calc^0 > 0.5 }

							check_variable = { influence_array^1 = CZE }
							check_variable = { influence_array_calc^1 > 0.5 }

							check_variable = { influence_array^2 = CZE }
							check_variable = { influence_array_calc^2 > 0.5 }

							check_variable = { influence_array^3 = CZE }
							check_variable = { influence_array_calc^3 > 0.5 }

							check_variable = { influence_array^4 = CZE }
							check_variable = { influence_array_calc^4 > 0.5 }

							check_variable = { influence_array^5 = CZE }
							check_variable = { influence_array_calc^5 > 0.5 }

							check_variable = { influence_array^6 = CZE }
							check_variable = { influence_array_calc^6 > 0.5 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			#EST = {
			#	
			#}
			country_exists = EST
		}

		visible = {
			EST = {
				has_opinion_modifier = threesi_member_modifier
				OR = {
					has_idea = CZ_unofficial_TSI_member
					has_idea = CZ_TSI_member
				}
			}
			has_completed_focus = czechia_TSI_convince
			country_exists = EST
			EST = {
				OR = {
					tag = PREV
					AND = {
						set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
						any_of = {
							array = influence_array
							value = v
							index = i
							if = {
								limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
								set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
								always = yes
							}
							else = { always = no }
						}
						check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx < 0.70 }
					}
					NOT = {
						check_variable = { influence_array^0 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^0 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^1 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^1 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^2 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^2 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^3 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^3 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^4 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^4 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^5 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^5 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^6 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^6 > 0.5 }
					}
				}
			}
		}

		cost = 50
		days_remove = 20
		days_re_enable = 1
		fire_only_once = no

		modifier = {
            political_power_gain = -0.50
        }

		remove_effect = {
			EST = {
				hidden_effect = {
					set_temp_variable = { influence_gain = 40 }
					for_loop_effect = {
						end = influence_array^num
						value = v
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { influence_array^v = CZE }
							}
							add_to_variable = { influence_array_val^v = influence_gain }
							set_country_flag = found
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = found } }
							add_to_array = { influence_array = CZE.id }
							add_to_array = { influence_array_val = influence_gain }
					}
					clr_country_flag = found
					recalculate_influence = yes
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = small_influence_40_tt
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 200
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_COMMUNIST
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_NATIONALIST
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_JIHADISTS
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_NEUTRALITY
				}
				factor = 5000
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = DEFAULT
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}

							index = i
							if = {
								limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
								set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
								always = yes
							}
							else = { always = no }
						}
						check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx < 0.70 }
					}
					NOT = {
						check_variable = { influence_array^0 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^0 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^1 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^1 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^2 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^2 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^3 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^3 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^4 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^4 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^5 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^5 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^6 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^6 > 0.5 }
					}
				}
			}
			has_completed_focus = czechia_TSI_convince
			country_exists = LIT
		}

		cost = 50
		days_remove = 20
		days_re_enable = 1
		fire_only_once = no

		modifier = {
            political_power_gain = -0.50
        }

		remove_effect = {
			LIT = {
				hidden_effect = {
					set_temp_variable = { influence_gain = 40 }
					for_loop_effect = {
						end = influence_array^num
						value = v
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { influence_array^v = CZE }
							}
							add_to_variable = { influence_array_val^v = influence_gain }
							set_country_flag = found
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = found } }
							add_to_array = { influence_array = CZE.id }
							add_to_array = { influence_array_val = influence_gain }
					}
					clr_country_flag = found
					recalculate_influence = yes
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = small_influence_40_tt
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 200
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_COMMUNIST
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_NATIONALIST
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_JIHADISTS
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_NEUTRALITY
				}
				factor = 5000
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = DEFAULT
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}

								limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
								set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
								always = yes
							}
							else = { always = no }
						}
						check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx < 0.70 }
					}
					NOT = {
						check_variable = { influence_array^0 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^0 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^1 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^1 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^2 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^2 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^3 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^3 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^4 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^4 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^5 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^5 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^6 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^6 > 0.5 }
					}
				}
			}
			has_completed_focus = czechia_TSI_convince
			country_exists = SLV
		}

		cost = 50
		days_remove = 20
		days_re_enable = 1
		fire_only_once = no

		modifier = {
            political_power_gain = -0.50
        }

		remove_effect = {
			SLV = {
				hidden_effect = {
					set_temp_variable = { influence_gain = 40 }
					for_loop_effect = {
						end = influence_array^num
						value = v
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { influence_array^v = CZE }
							}
							add_to_variable = { influence_array_val^v = influence_gain }
							set_country_flag = found
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = found } }
							add_to_array = { influence_array = CZE.id }
							add_to_array = { influence_array_val = influence_gain }
					}
					clr_country_flag = found
					recalculate_influence = yes
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = small_influence_40_tt
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 200
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_COMMUNIST
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_NATIONALIST
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_JIHADISTS
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_NEUTRALITY
				}
				factor = 5000
			}
			modifier = {

							else = { always = no }
						}
						check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx < 0.70 }
					}
					NOT = {
						check_variable = { influence_array^0 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^0 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^1 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^1 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^2 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^2 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^3 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^3 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^4 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^4 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^5 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^5 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^6 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^6 > 0.5 }
					}
				}
			}
			has_completed_focus = czechia_TSI_convince
			country_exists = BUL
		}

		cost = 50
		days_remove = 20
		days_re_enable = 1
		fire_only_once = no

		modifier = {
            political_power_gain = -0.50
        }

		remove_effect = {
			BUL = {
				hidden_effect = {
					set_temp_variable = { influence_gain = 40 }
					for_loop_effect = {
						end = influence_array^num
						value = v
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { influence_array^v = CZE }
							}
							add_to_variable = { influence_array_val^v = influence_gain }
							set_country_flag = found
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = found } }
							add_to_array = { influence_array = CZE.id }
							add_to_array = { influence_array_val = influence_gain }
					}
					clr_country_flag = found
					recalculate_influence = yes
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = small_influence_40_tt
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 200
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_COMMUNIST
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_NATIONALIST
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_JIHADISTS
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_NEUTRALITY
				}
				factor = 5000
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = DEFAULT
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}

			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = var:czechia_new1_capital
			}

		}


		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = czechia_is_leader_of_TSI
				has_country_flag = official_leader_of_TSI
			}
			var:czechia_new_TSI_member1 = {
				has_opinion_modifier = threesi_member_modifier
			}
			has_government = neutrality
			political_power_daily > 0.5
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = required_not_70_influence_new1
				var:czechia_new_TSI_member1 = {
					OR = {
						tag = PREV
						AND = {
							set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
							any_of = {
								array = influence_array
								value = v
								index = i
								if = {
									limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
									set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
									always = yes
								}
								else = { always = no }
							}
							check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
							check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx < 0.70 }

			var:czechia_new_TSI_member4 = {
				has_opinion_modifier = threesi_member_modifier
				OR = {
					has_idea = CZ_unofficial_TSI_member
					has_idea = CZ_TSI_member
				}
			}
			var:czechia_new_TSI_member4 = {
				OR = {
					tag = PREV
					AND = {
						set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
						any_of = {
							array = influence_array
							value = v
							index = i
							if = {
								limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
								set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
								always = yes
							}
							else = { always = no }
						}
						check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx < 0.70 }
					}
					NOT = {
						check_variable = { influence_array^0 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^0 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^1 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^1 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^2 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^2 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^3 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^3 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^4 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^4 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^5 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^5 > 0.5 }

						check_variable = { influence_array^6 = CZE }
						check_variable = { influence_array_calc^6 > 0.5 }
					}
				}
			}
			has_completed_focus = czechia_TSI_convince
			country_exists = var:czechia_new_TSI_member4
		}

		cost = 50
		days_remove = 20
		days_re_enable = 1
		fire_only_once = no

		modifier = {
            political_power_gain = -0.50
        }

		remove_effect = {
			var:czechia_new_TSI_member4 = {
				hidden_effect = {
					set_temp_variable = { influence_gain = 40 }
					for_loop_effect = {
						end = influence_array^num
						value = v
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { influence_array^v = CZE }
							}
							add_to_variable = { influence_array_val^v = influence_gain }
							set_country_flag = found
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = found } }
							add_to_array = { influence_array = CZE.id }
							add_to_array = { influence_array_val = influence_gain }
					}
					clr_country_flag = found
					recalculate_influence = yes
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = small_influence_40_tt
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 200
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_COMMUNIST
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_NATIONALIST
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_JIHADISTS
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_NEUTRALITY
				}
				factor = 5000
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = DEFAULT
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}

	czech_TSI_neu_create_fac_est = {

		icon = faction_dec

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = var:czechia_est_capital
			}
			highlight_color_while_active = 2
		}


		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = czechia_is_leader_of_TSI
				has_country_flag = official_leader_of_TSI
			}
			political_power_daily > 0.5
			has_government = neutrality
			EST = {
				has_opinion_modifier = threesi_member_modifier
			}
			country_exists = EST
			EST = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = CZ_TSI_aliance
					has_war_with = FROM
					CZE = {
						has_wargoal_against = PREV
					}
				}
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = czechia_influence_above50_est_tt
					OR = {
						tag = PREV
						AND = {
							set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
							any_of = {
								array = influence_array
								value = v
								index = i
								if = {
									limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
									set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
									always = yes
								}
								else = { always = no }
							}
							check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
							check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.50 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = czechia_TSI_faction
			country_exists = EST
			EST = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = CZ_TSI_aliance
					has_war_with = FROM
					CZE = {
						has_wargoal_against = PREV
					}
				}
				has_idea = CZ_unofficial_TSI_member
			}
		}

		cost = 10
		days_remove = 20
		days_re_enable = 1
		fire_only_once = no

		modifier = {
            political_power_gain = -0.50
        }

		remove_effect = {
			EST = {
				country_event = { id = czechia.50 }	
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 200
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_COMMUNIST
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_JIHADISTS
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_NATIONALIST
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_NEUTRALITY
				}
				factor = 5000
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = DEFAULT
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}

			EST = {

				NOT = {
					has_war_with = CZE
					is_subject_of = CZE
				}
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = czechia_influence_above60_est_tt

									always = yes
								}
								else = { always = no }
							}
							check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
							check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.60 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {

				NOT = {
					has_war_with = CZE
					is_subject_of = CZE
				}
				has_idea = CZ_TSI_member
			}
		}

		cost = 10
		days_remove = 20
		days_re_enable = 1
		fire_only_once = no

		modifier = {
            political_power_gain = -0.50
        }

		remove_effect = {
			EST = {
				CZE = {
					puppet = PREV
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_opinion_modifier = threesi_member_modifier
						}
					}
					EST = {
						add_opinion_modifier = {
						    target = FROM
						    modifier = threesi_member_modifier
						}
					}
					add_opinion_modifier = {
					    target = EST
					    modifier = threesi_member_modifier
					}
				}
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_COMMUNIST
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_JIHADISTS
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR

				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {

				tooltip = czechia_is_leader_of_TSI
				has_country_flag = official_leader_of_TSI
			}
			political_power_daily > 0.5
			AUS = {
				has_opinion_modifier = threesi_member_modifier
			}
			has_government = neutrality
			has_idea = CZ_TSI_aliance
			AUS = {
				has_idea = CZ_TSI_aliance
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = CZE
					is_subject_of = CZE
				}
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = czechia_influence_above60_aus_tt
					OR = {
						tag = PREV
						AND = {
							set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
							any_of = {
								array = influence_array
								value = v
								index = i
								if = {
									limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
									set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
									always = yes
								}
								else = { always = no }
							}
							check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
							check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.60 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = czechia_TSI_integrate
			has_idea = CZ_TSI_aliance
			country_exists = AUS
			AUS = {
				has_idea = CZ_TSI_aliance
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = CZE
					is_subject_of = CZE
				}
				has_idea = CZ_TSI_member
			}
		}

		cost = 10
		days_remove = 20
		days_re_enable = 1
		fire_only_once = no

		modifier = {
            political_power_gain = -0.50
        }

		remove_effect = {
			AUS = {
				CZE = {
					puppet = PREV
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_opinion_modifier = threesi_member_modifier
						}
					}
					AUS = {
						add_opinion_modifier = {
						    target = FROM
						    modifier = threesi_member_modifier
						}
					}
					add_opinion_modifier = {
					    target = AUS
					    modifier = threesi_member_modifier
					}
				}
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_COMMUNIST
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_JIHADISTS
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_NATIONALIST
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_NEUTRALITY
				}
				factor = 5000
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = DEFAULT
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}

			}

			var:czechia_new_TSI_member2 = {
				has_opinion_modifier = threesi_member_modifier
			}
			has_government = neutrality
			has_idea = CZ_TSI_aliance
			var:czechia_new_TSI_member2 = {
				has_idea = CZ_TSI_aliance
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = CZE
					is_subject_of = CZE
				}
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = czechia_influence_above60_new2_tt
					OR = {
						tag = PREV
						AND = {
							set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
							any_of = {
								array = influence_array
								value = v
								index = i
								if = {
									limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
									set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
									always = yes
								}
								else = { always = no }
							}
							check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
							check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.60 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = czechia_TSI_integrate
			has_idea = CZ_TSI_aliance
			country_exists = var:czechia_new_TSI_member2
			var:czechia_new_TSI_member2 = {
				has_idea = CZ_TSI_aliance
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = CZE
					is_subject_of = CZE
				}
				has_idea = CZ_TSI_member
			}
		}

		cost = 10
		days_remove = 20
		days_re_enable = 1
		fire_only_once = no

		modifier = {
            political_power_gain = -0.50
        }

		remove_effect = {
			var:czechia_new_TSI_member2 = {
				CZE = {
					puppet = PREV
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_opinion_modifier = threesi_member_modifier
						}
					}
					var:czechia_new_TSI_member2 = {

						    target = FROM
						    modifier = threesi_member_modifier
						}
						FROM = {
							add_opinion_modifier = {
								target = PREV
								modifier = threesi_member_modifier
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {

			modifier = {

				}

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = var:czechia_est_capital
			}

		}


		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = czechia_is_leader_of_TSI
				has_country_flag = official_leader_of_TSI
			}
			political_power_daily > 0.5
			EST = {
				has_opinion_modifier = threesi_member_modifier
			}
			has_government = neutrality
			has_idea = CZ_TSI_aliance
			EST = {
				has_idea = CZ_TSI_aliance
				is_subject_of = CZE
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = czechia_influence_above70_est_tt
					OR = {
						tag = PREV
						AND = {
							set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
							any_of = {
								array = influence_array
								value = v
								index = i
								if = {
									limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
									set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
									always = yes
								}
								else = { always = no }
							}
							check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
							check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.70 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = czechia_TSI_integrate
			has_idea = CZ_TSI_aliance
			country_exists = EST
			EST = {
				has_idea = CZ_TSI_aliance
				has_idea = CZ_TSI_member
				is_subject_of = CZE
			}
		}

		cost = 10
		days_remove = 20
		days_re_enable = 1
		fire_only_once = no

		modifier = {
            political_power_gain = -0.50
        }

		remove_effect = {
			EST = {
				CZE = {
					annex_country = {
						target = PREV
						transfer_troops = yes
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = EST
						NOT = { owner = { tag = CZE } }
					}
					EST = {
						remove_state_core = PREV
					}
					CZE = {
						add_state_core = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 200
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_COMMUNIST
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_JIHADISTS
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_NATIONALIST
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_NEUTRALITY
				}
				factor = 5000
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = DEFAULT
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}

		icon = annex_dec

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = var:czechia_pol_capital
			}
			highlight_color_while_active = 1
		}


		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = czechia_is_leader_of_TSI
				has_country_flag = official_leader_of_TSI
			}
			political_power_daily > 0.5
			POL = {
				has_opinion_modifier = threesi_member_modifier
			}
			has_government = neutrality
			has_idea = CZ_TSI_aliance
			POL = {
				has_idea = CZ_TSI_aliance
				is_subject_of = CZE
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = czechia_influence_above70_pol_tt
					OR = {
						tag = PREV
						AND = {
							set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
							any_of = {
								array = influence_array
								value = v
								index = i
								if = {
									limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
									set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
									always = yes
								}
								else = { always = no }
							}
							check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
							check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.70 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = czechia_TSI_integrate
			has_idea = CZ_TSI_aliance
			country_exists = POL
			POL = {
				has_idea = CZ_TSI_aliance
				has_idea = CZ_TSI_member
				is_subject_of = CZE
			}
		}

		cost = 10
		days_remove = 20
		days_re_enable = 1
		fire_only_once = no

		modifier = {
            political_power_gain = -0.50
        }

		remove_effect = {
			POL = {
				CZE = {
					annex_country = {
						target = PREV
						transfer_troops = yes
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = POL
						NOT = { owner = { tag = CZE } }
					}
					POL = {
						remove_state_core = PREV
					}
					CZE = {
						add_state_core = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 200
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_COMMUNIST
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_JIHADISTS
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_NATIONALIST
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_NEUTRALITY
				}
				factor = 5000
			}
			modifier = {

	czech_TSI_annex_bul = {

		icon = annex_dec

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = var:czechia_bul_capital
			}
			highlight_color_while_active = 1
		}


		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = czechia_is_leader_of_TSI
				has_country_flag = official_leader_of_TSI
			}
			political_power_daily > 0.5
			BUL = {
				has_opinion_modifier = threesi_member_modifier
			}
			has_government = neutrality
			has_idea = CZ_TSI_aliance
			BUL = {
				has_idea = CZ_TSI_aliance
				is_subject_of = CZE
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = czechia_influence_above70_bul_tt
					OR = {
						tag = PREV
						AND = {
							set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = -1 }
							any_of = {
								array = influence_array
								value = v
								index = i
								if = {
									limit = { var:v = { tag = ROOT } }
									set_temp_variable = { temp_idx = i }
									always = yes
								}
								else = { always = no }
							}
							check_variable = { temp_idx > -1 }
							check_variable = { influence_array_calc^temp_idx > 0.70 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = czechia_TSI_integrate
			has_idea = CZ_TSI_aliance
			country_exists = BUL
			BUL = {
				has_idea = CZ_TSI_aliance
				has_idea = CZ_TSI_member
				is_subject_of = CZE
			}
		}

		cost = 10
		days_remove = 20
		days_re_enable = 1
		fire_only_once = no

		modifier = {
            political_power_gain = -0.50
        }

		remove_effect = {
			BUL = {
				CZE = {
					annex_country = {
						target = PREV
						transfer_troops = yes
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = BUL
						NOT = { owner = { tag = CZE } }
					}
					BUL = {
						remove_state_core = PREV
					}
					CZE = {
						add_state_core = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 200
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_COMMUNIST
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_JIHADISTS
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_NATIONALIST
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = CZE_NEUTRALITY
				}
				factor = 5000
			}
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = Czech_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = DEFAULT
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}

					}
				}

	czech_TSI_group = {

		icon = 3si_dec

		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = czechia_is_leader_of_TSI
				has_country_flag = official_leader_of_TSI
			}
			political_power_daily > 2
			has_government = neutrality
			NOT = {
				country_exists = POL
				country_exists = HUN
				country_exists = SLO
				country_exists = AUS
				country_exists = CRO
				country_exists = SLV
				country_exists = ROM
				country_exists = BUL
				country_exists = LIT
				country_exists = LAT
				country_exists = EST
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = czechia_all_TSI_tt
				all_state = {
					OR = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = POL }
						AND = {
							is_core_of = POL
							owner = { tag = CZE }
						}
					}
				}
				all_state = {
					OR = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = HUN }
						AND = {
							is_core_of = HUN
							owner = { tag = CZE }
						}

cz_TSI_group_kicks_category = {
	czech_TSI_kick = {

		#icon = annex_dec

		target_trigger = {
			FROM ={
				NOT = {
					original_tag = SOV
					original_tag = CHI
					original_tag = ROOT
				}
				OR = {
					has_idea = CZ_TSI_member
					has_idea = CZ_unofficial_TSI_member
				}
			}
		}


		available = {
			political_power_daily > 0.5
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = czechia_TSI_kicks_shown
			has_country_flag = official_leader_of_TSI
			OR = {
				original_tag = CZE
				original_tag = SLO
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = czechia_TSI_kick_in_process }
		}

		cost = 50
		days_remove = 1
		days_re_enable = 1
		fire_only_once = no

		modifier = {
            political_power_gain = -0.50
        }
		
		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				ROOT = { set_country_flag = { flag = czechia_TSI_kick_in_process days = 1 value = 1 } }
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			FROM = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = { czechia_new_TSI_member1 = FROM.id }
							check_variable = { czechia_new_TSI_member2 = FROM.id }
							check_variable = { czechia_new_TSI_member3 = FROM.id }
							check_variable = { czechia_new_TSI_member4 = FROM.id }
						}
					}
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								has_idea = CZ_TSI_aliance
								has_idea = CZ_TSI_member
								has_idea = CZ_unofficial_TSI_member
							}
							NOT = {
								original_tag = PREV
							}
						}
						#hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = czechia.55 } }
						hidden_effect = { CZE_calculate_number_of_v4_or_TSI_members = yes }
						if = {
							limit = {
								PREV = {
									check_variable = { czechia_new_TSI_member1 = FROM.id }
								}
							}
							clear_variable = czechia_new_TSI_member1
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								PREV = {
									check_variable = { czechia_new_TSI_member2 = FROM.id }
								}
							}
							clear_variable = czechia_new_TSI_member2
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								PREV = {
									check_variable = { czechia_new_TSI_member3 = FROM.id }
								}
							}
							clear_variable = czechia_new_TSI_member3
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								PREV = {
									check_variable = { czechia_new_TSI_member4 = FROM.id }
								}
							}
							clear_variable = czechia_new_TSI_member4
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { czechia_new_TSI_member1 = FROM.id }
						}
						clear_variable = czechia_new_TSI_member1
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { czechia_new_TSI_member2 = FROM.id }
						}
						clear_variable = czechia_new_TSI_member2
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { czechia_new_TSI_member3 = FROM.id }
						}
						clear_variable = czechia_new_TSI_member3
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { czechia_new_TSI_member4 = FROM.id }
						}
						clear_variable = czechia_new_TSI_member4
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = CZ_TSI_aliance
					}
					left_TSI = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = CZ_TSI_member
					}
					remove_ideas = CZ_TSI_member
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = CZ_unofficial_TSI_member
					}
					remove_ideas = CZ_unofficial_TSI_member
				}
				clear_variable = czechia_TSI_members_number
			}
			hidden_effect = { 
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_idea = CZ_TSI_aliance
							has_idea = CZ_TSI_member
							has_idea = CZ_unofficial_TSI_member
						}
					}
					#country_event = { id = czechia.55 }
					CZE_calculate_number_of_v4_or_TSI_members = yes
				}
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 1

			modifier = {
				ROOT = { has_opinion = { target = FROM value > 0 } }
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				ROOT = { has_opinion = { target = FROM value < 0 } }
				factor = 1
			}
			modifier = {
				ROOT = { has_opinion = { target = FROM value < -25 } }
				factor = 1.5
			}
			modifier = {
				ROOT = { has_opinion = { target = FROM value < -50 }}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				ROOT = {
					OR = {
						any_enemy_country = {
							is_in_faction_with = FROM
						}
						any_allied_country = {
							has_war_with = FROM
						}
					}
				}
				add = 100
				factor = 10
			}
		}
	}
}

				}
			}

        }

		days_re_enable = 1

				set_country_flag = czechia_AZ_dec_dissolved
			}
			if = { limit = { defence_02_or_01 = yes }
				set_country_flag = czechia_AZ_dec_default
			}
			if = { limit = { defence_04_or_03 = yes }
				set_country_flag = czechia_upgrade_1_AZ_dec_upgrade1
			}
        }

		complete_effect = {

		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 200
		}
	}

cz_highway_category = {
	czech_maintenance_of_highway = {
		icon = highway_dec
		visible = {
			any_controlled_state = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = czech_highways }
			}
		}
		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_war = yes
			}
		}
		cost = 150
		days_remove = 730
		days_re_enable = 60
	
		ai_will_do = { base = 0 }
	
		complete_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -20 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
		}

		remove_effect = {
			every_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = czech_highways }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = czech_highways } 
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			political_power_gain = -0.1
		}
	}
	czech_sabotage_highway = {
		icon = highway_dec
		visible = {
			NOT = {
				any_controlled_state = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = czech_highways }
				}
			}
			OR = {
				controls_state = 117
				controls_state = 118
				controls_state = 1017
				controls_state = 1018
			}
			has_war = yes
		}
		available = {
			OR = {
				controls_state = 117
				controls_state = 118
				controls_state = 1017
				controls_state = 1018
			}
			has_war = yes
		}
		cost = 300
		days_remove = 90
		days_re_enable = 60
	
		ai_will_do = { base = 0 }
	
		complete_effect = {
			if = { limit = { controls_state = 117 } 117 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = czech_highways_sabotaged } } }
			if = { limit = { controls_state = 118 } 118 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = czech_highways_sabotaged } } }
			if = { limit = { controls_state = 1017 } 1017 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = czech_highways_sabotaged } } }
			if = { limit = { controls_state = 1018 } 1018 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = czech_highways_sabotaged } } }
		}

		remove_effect = {
			if = { limit = { 117 = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = czech_highways_sabotaged } } } 117 = { remove_dynamic_modifier  = { modifier = czech_highways_sabotaged } } }
			if = { limit = { 118 = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = czech_highways_sabotaged } } } 118 = { remove_dynamic_modifier  = { modifier = czech_highways_sabotaged } } }
			if = { limit = { 1017 = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = czech_highways_sabotaged } } } 1017 = { remove_dynamic_modifier  = { modifier = czech_highways_sabotaged } } }
			if = { limit = { 1018 = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = czech_highways_sabotaged } } } 1018 = { remove_dynamic_modifier  = { modifier = czech_highways_sabotaged } } }
		}
	}
}

					add_to_variable = { Excalibur_Army_decision = 1 }

				add_to_variable = { Excalibur_Army_decision_overtime = 1 }

				set_variable = { temp_CSG_investment_days = 45 }

				initialize_czechoslovak_group_dynamic_modifiers = yes
			}
			SLO = {
				set_temp_variable = { Excalibur_Army_decision_kys = Excalibur_Army_decision }
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { Excalibur_Army_decision = 4 } } }
					add_to_temp_variable = { Excalibur_Army_decision_kys = 1 }
					add_to_variable = { Excalibur_Army_decision = 1 }

				set_variable = { temp_CSG_investment_days = 45 }

				initialize_czechoslovak_group_dynamic_modifiers = yes
			}
		}

			factor = 1
		}

		}

					limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { DAKO_CZ_decision = 5 } } }
					add_to_temp_variable = { DAKO_CZ_decision_kys = 1 }
					add_to_variable = { DAKO_CZ_decision = 1 }
				}
				add_to_variable = { DAKO_CZ_decision_overtime = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { DAKO_CZ = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -1 }
				set_variable = { temp_CSG_investment_days = 45 }
				modify_treasury_effect = yes
				initialize_czechoslovak_group_dynamic_modifiers = yes
			}
			SLO = {
				set_temp_variable = { DAKO_CZ_decision_kys = DAKO_CZ_decision }

				set_temp_variable = { LAND_SYSTEMS_decision_kys = LAND_SYSTEMS_decision }
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { LAND_SYSTEMS_decision = 4 } } }
					add_to_temp_variable = { LAND_SYSTEMS_decision_kys = 1 }
					add_to_variable = { LAND_SYSTEMS_decision = 1 }
				}
				add_to_variable = { LAND_SYSTEMS_decision_overtime = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { LAND_SYSTEMS = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -1 }
				set_variable = { temp_CSG_investment_days = 45 }
				modify_treasury_effect = yes
				initialize_czechoslovak_group_dynamic_modifiers = yes
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
